			<header class="entry-header">

						<a href="https://highjewellerydream.com/category/high-jewellery-2/" rel="category tag">High Jewellery</a> <a href="https://highjewellerydream.com/category/in-the-news/" rel="category tag">In The News</a> <a href="https://highjewellerydream.com/category/jewellery-stories/" rel="category tag">Jewellery Stories</a>					</div><!-- end .entry-cats -->
								<h2 class="entry-title"><a href="https://highjewellerydream.com/empress-eugenie-crown-restoration-louvre/" rel="bookmark">From Damage to Preservation: The Restoration of Empress Eugénie’s Crown at the Louvre</a></h2>			</header><!-- end .entry-header -->
			<div class="entry-summary">
				<p>Damaged during the October 2025 robbery at the Louvre yet miraculously spared from loss, the crown of Empress Eugénie is now at the heart of an exceptional restoration project. Nearly intact and rich in historical symbolism, the restoration of Empress Eugénie’s crown marks a new chapter of preservation, expertise, and cultural memory.</p>
			</div><!-- .entry-summary -->

		<div class="entry-main">
			<header class="entry-header">
									<div class="entry-cats">
						<a href="https://highjewellerydream.com/category/chanel/" rel="category tag">Chanel</a> <a href="https://highjewellerydream.com/category/chanel-timepieces/" rel="category tag">Chanel Timepieces</a> <a href="https://highjewellerydream.com/category/fine-jewellery/" rel="category tag">fine jewellery</a>					</div><!-- end .entry-cats -->
								<h2 class="entry-title"><a href="https://highjewellerydream.com/chanel-from-dream-to-reality-a-winter-tale-of-watches-and-fine-jewellery/" rel="bookmark">CHANEL &#8211; “From Dream to Reality”: A Winter Tale of Watches and Fine Jewellery</a></h2>			</header><!-- end .entry-header -->
			<div class="entry-summary">
				<p>CHANEL reveals “From Dream to Reality,” a poetic winter campaign where wishes take form in the snow. Featuring Mona Tougaard and Rebecca Leigh, the Maison’s iconic J12, Première, Coco Crush and Camélia creations illuminate a dreamlike world of light, symbols and timeless elegance.</p>
			</div><!-- .entry-summary -->

	<div class="entry-summary">
		<p>Saved for the nation after an extraordinary fundraising campaign, the Tudor Heart Pendant — a rare 16th-century jewel linked to the marriage of Henry VIII and Catherine of Aragon — now enters the British Museum collection.</p>
